***recessie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:recessie.html>recessie</a> (29703)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Zyyy mention" lang="und">recess</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:-ie.html>-ie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">recessus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a going back, retreat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">recessum</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">recedere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to recede</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:re-.html>re-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">back</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cedere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recessie.html>recessie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recessie.html>recessies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recessie.html>recessietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">economic</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">recession</span></li></ol>

***recht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a> (564)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">reht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rehtaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃reǵtós</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechter.html>rechter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">rechtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>right (direction)</li>
<li>straight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">in <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:rechte.html>rechte</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:lijn.html>lijn</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">in a straight line</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krom.html>krom</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">reht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rehtą</i>, a substantive derivation of the adjective.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechten.html>rechten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>rechtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a right, privilege
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> have the <b>right</b> to do that!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>justice
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:noemt.html>Noemt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></b>? <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noem.html>noem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onrecht.html>onrecht</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you call this <b>justice</b>? I call this injustice.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloer.html>vloer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This boring floor doesn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> do the house any <b>justice</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>jurisprudence, the law
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:omtrent.html>omtrent</a> cybercriminaliteit <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:momenteel.html>momenteel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onduidelijk.html>onduidelijk</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Jurisprudence</b> concerning cybercrime <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> currently still very unclear.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beslist.html>beslist</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b>law</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> decided.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***rechten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rechten.html>rechten</a> (2090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">(what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>) right, justice, law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>Recht</a></i>, also from the adjective <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right, straight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
<span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium. Particularly: “aren’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> that 2 etymologies? Transform pedia quote below to etymology.”)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechten.html>rechten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>To seek justice, notably:
<ol><li>To sue judicially</li>
<li>To contend by argument etc.</li></ol></li>
<li>To straighten</li>
<li>To erect, raise</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">seek justice</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoeken.html>zoeken</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">seek justice<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> judicial only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:procederen.html>procederen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">straighten</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">rechtmaken</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechttrekken.html>rechttrekken</a></span> (both cognate)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">erect</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oprichten.html>oprichten</a></span> (cognate)</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechten.html>rechten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">academic subject<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> law
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitdrukking.html>uitdrukking</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:rechten.html>rechten</a></b>’ <a href = vnd.unilang:stamt.html>stamt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:universitair.html>universitair</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderwijs.html>onderwijs</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middeleeuwen.html>middeleeuwen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toen.html>toen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:juridische.html>juridische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:faculteiten.html>faculteiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zowel.html>zowel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereldlijk.html>wereldlijk</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> Romeins) <a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> canoniek <a href = vnd.unilang:recht.html>recht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:studeren.html>studeren</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rechtsgeleerdheid">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>The appellation ‘<b>laws</b>’ derives from the university-level education in the middle ages, when at the law colleges one could study secular (mainly Roman) law as well as canon law.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rechtsgang.html>rechtsgang</a> (18361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechtsgang.html>rechtsgang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:rechtsgang.html>rechtsgang</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rechts.html>rechts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***recidivist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:recidivist.html>recidivist</a> (56179)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">récidiviste</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">recidīvus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">returning, recurring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">recidivous</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ist</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:recidivist.html>recidivist</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">recidivists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who falls back into prior habits, especially criminal habits.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">repeat offender</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1914</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/R._Austin_Freeman" class="extiw" title="w:R. Austin Freeman"><a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>R</a>. Austin Freeman</a>, <i>The Uttermost Farthing</i>, ch. 2:
<dl><dd>This specimen <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> of English parentage, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a professional burglar, a confirmed <b><a href = vnd.unilang:recidivist.html>recidivist</a></b>, and—since he habitually carried firearms—a potential homicide.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:rectum.html>rectum</a></i>, abbreviation of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:rectum.html>rectum</a> intestinum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the straight intestine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:rectum.html>rectum</a></i>, neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rectus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">straight</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***redcap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>redcap</a> (73306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">red</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cap</i>.
</p><p>In sense of "<a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a>", 1890s US; compare contemporary <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">赤帽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">akabou</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. On Labor Day, 1890, John Williams,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> an African-American railway <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a>, tied a red ribbon to his black <a href = vnd.unilang:uniform.html>uniform</a> cap to stand out from the crowd at Grand Central Terminal. The strategy <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so successful that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> soon adopted by others in the profession, leading to the synecdochic use of <a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>redcap</a> as a term for all railway <a href = vnd.unilang:porters.html>porters</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>redcap</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">redcaps</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A member of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Royal_Military_Police" class="extiw" title="w:Royal Military Police">Royal Military Police</a> a unit in the British army.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>porter</a> in a US railway station.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The European goldfinch (<i>Carduelis carduelis</i>).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> folklore</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A type of evil <a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a> or imp.
<ul><li><b>1876:</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:porter.html>Porter</a> amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:coates.html>Coates</a> (pub.), <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?vid=0xX5AYwnNuW_isE9h9amp;id=D9zaWVMVnMwCamp;pg=PA450amp;lpg=PA450amp;dq=%22redcap%22amp;as_brr=1">Reliques of Ancient English Poetry</a></i>
<dl><dd>Lord Soulis he <a href = vnd.unilang:sat.html>sat</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>Hermitage</a> Castle,</dd>
<dd>And beside him Old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>Redcap</a></b> sly;  | </dd>
<dd>"Now, tell <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, thou sprite, who are meikle of might,</dd>
<dd>The death that I must <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>?"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1890:</b> Joseph Jacobs, <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com/books?vid=OCLC04286010amp;id=IZvGIR27HLcCamp;pg=PA204amp;lpg=PA204amp;dq=%22redcap%22amp;as_brr=1">English Fairy Tales</a></i>
<dl><dd>"What's a Brownie?" you say. <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, it's a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of a sort of a Bogle, but it isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> so cruel as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>Redcap</a></b>! What! you don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know what's a Bogle or a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>Redcap</a></b>!</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2002:</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:cecilia.html>Cecilia</a> Dart-Thornton, <i>The Ill-Made Mute: The Bitterbynde</i> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?vid=ISBN0446610801amp;id=htuFPpu6NoECamp;pg=PA453amp;lpg=PA453amp;dq=redcap+goblinamp;sig=uM3txbLAAyZm8Ukii0ma_9wzsKMamp;hl=en">[1]</a>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> the <a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> aroused the mercenary's ire. This seemed to bring out a formidable and hitherto unrecognized <a href = vnd.unilang:talent.html>talent</a> in the taciturn young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</dd>
<dd>"Why cam' ye by my <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>?" The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>redcap</a></b> brandished his pikestaff menacingly.</dd>
<dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:redcap.html>Redcap</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> A malevolent <a href = vnd.unilang:goblin.html>goblin</a> easily distinguishable by their namesake red cap, fiery red <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>, claws and iron boots. They often appear as little old <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a>, but can run very fast despite the boots. They reside in castles and watchtowers along the English-Scottish border, but will move their residence to avoid detection. They have sharp eagle’s <a href = vnd.unilang:talons.html>talons</a> which they use for <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>weapons</a>, but can easily be repelled simply by reading holy verse. <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.vf11.com/legendsofvalhal/legendsofvalhal-post-814.html">[2]</a></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1999</b>, J. K. Rowling, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>Harry</a> Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</i>
<dl><dd>After boggarts, they studied <b>Red <a href = vnd.unilang:caps.html>Caps</a></b>, nasty little goblinlike <a href = vnd.unilang:creatures.html>creatures</a> that lurked where there <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> bloodshed <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A breed of poultry.
<dl><dd>Red Cap: A <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> member of the English class, these are characterized by having a large <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> comb. They are one of the few breeds with red earlobes that lay white-shelled eggs. Content: Chicken Breeds and Varieties (A2880), John L. <a href = vnd.unilang:skinner.html>Skinner</a>, University of Wisconsin-Madison <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20060907060926/http://www.ansi.okstate.edu/poultry/chickens/redcap/">[3]</a></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>
